## Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre

We are one of the largest gyms, swim schools, and group fitness providers in the Glenelg Shire. Offering you the largest swimming and water safety program to ensure kids are set with a skill for life.

# Welcome to the Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre

The Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre (PLACE) aims to provide an enjoyable experience for the whole community, both members or guests to participate and use any of our services, programs and activities. We offer the largest Swimming and Water Safety program in the area helping kids Learn to Swim all year round.

The Health Club has a large gym facility which is fully equipped with a variety of weights, machines and cardio equipment. We pride ourselves with our Group Fitness offering, hosting 8 Auqa classes, 18 Reformer Pilates classes and 37 other mixed classes a week. That's a total of 63 classes a week!!

PLACE has something for the whole family to enjoy, whether it be a leisurely day around one of our five swimming pools or enjoying coffee at the Café after your workout. We look forward to offering you the best health and leisure experience possible. 

Come in and visit us today to see what PLACE has to offer you!

## Opening Hours 

#### Mon – Fri:

6am to 8pm

10 Oct 25 

###  World Mental Health Day! 

World Mental Health Day is observed on 10 October each year as a global movement to raise awareness, reduce stigma, and encourage positive action for mental wellbeing. The day invites communities, workplaces, schools, and individuals to pause, reflect, and act in ways that strengthen social connection and mental health.  


[ Read More ](/news/world-mental-health-day)

01 Sep 25 

###  Say Yes to You: Make Time to Move 

It's Women’s Health Week 2025! Whether small or bold, every choice to move supports your physical, mental, and social wellbeing. Read more about the health tips to follow this week from our Group Health and Wellbeing Manager, Victoria Goodwin-Barlow, and our Allied Health Manager, Kia Naylor.  


[ Read More ](/news/say-yes-to-you-make-time-to-move)

# Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre welcome 350 at Tri State Games Aquatics Day 

27 Nov 2025 

Venue

Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre (PLACE) has proudly hosted Aquatics Day for the second year in a row as part of the 2025 Tri State Games. The annual, week-long, inclusive sporting event brings together over 300 athletes of all abilities from across Victoria, South Australia and New South Wales.   


Offering an opportunity for those living with disability across the three states to participate in sport, the Tri State games provide a stage to promote the athlete’s achievements within the community whilst providing an opportunity to improve their health, fitness and quality of life.   


Kyeema Support Services, Glenelg Shire Council, PLACE team members, local volunteers and service clubs were instrumental in facilitating the landmark event which celebrated a wide range of abilities.   


**_A day of inclusivity and connection_**

The games kicked off with a celebratory street parade and opening ceremony, and from 9:30 AM to 4:00 PM, energised spectators enthusiastically cheered on the athletes from the poolside. Freestyle, backstroke and butterfly races took place as well as across-the-pool challenges using kickboards, noodles and walking aids.   


The event – running from 11th to 14th November, featured athletics events, indoor sports and themed evening functions open for all to attend.   


Wanda, a PLACE spokesperson shared:   


“It was a pleasure to watch the energy in the pool today from all our participants. We’re so thrilled to be part of an event that celebrates ability and inclusive sport.”   


“Seeing the Tri State Games events come together reminded me why what we do is so important: our work helps connect everyone with sporting opportunities,” she continued.

Participant, Michael, shared:   


“I love the Tri State Games because I get to catch up with others at the event, travel to other states, make new friends, party every night and win medals! I won 3 medals – 2 bronze and 1 gold.” 

At PLACE, the team are honoured to support the Tri State Games’ mission of promoting inclusion and health for all athletes in the community once more, by offering a welcoming and inclusive environment for them to compete and thrive.

# GoAcademy

## GOswim Academy

Developed in partnership with industry experts, GOswim Academy forms a part of the GOswim program and is designed to increase participation in swimming in a fun and engaging way, helping kids across Australia develop their swimming skills further at a pace that’s right for them.  
  
Research has revealed that thousands of kids stop swimming because it stops being fun for them. Industry experts and the GOswim Academy program have developed a mixture of offerings to encourage continued participation in aquatic activity through competitive and reactional lap swimming.  
  
This is an exciting program where kids across Australia can have fun with their friends and improve their swimming in a safe, social and non-competitive environment.

## Join GOswim Academy

For more information the program or to express your interest please complete an enquiry form on our contact page. 

## The Curriculum

The curriculum for this program builds on the core and foundation elements learnt in swimming and water safety education, as each skill is broken down into segmented and achievable components that streamline and refine technique and enhance the development of efficiency and endurance.

### **Stage One**

Stage one is designed to continue the learning of new aquatic skills whilst refining those previously learnt swimming skills. Utilising them in a variety of simulated scenarios and aquatic disciplines.

### **Stage Two**

Stage two is designed to equip the student with all the skills required to become the swimmer they want to be. Skills included in the stage cover all aquatic disciplines, water safety and recreational swimming.

##  GOswim Academy FAQs Expand all 

#####  Who Does GOswim Academy Cater To? 

Aimed at kids who have already learnt the basics of swimming, GOswim Academy is designed for students aged between the ages of 8 and 14 years old. It’s perfect for kids ready for junior squads, or for those who are interested in getting ready for the competitive swimming club environment.

# Memberships and Passes

## 

## Start Your Journey Today

Join the Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre (PLACE) community with a membership designed to support your health and wellbeing goals. Our memberships provide access to all our facilities, including the gym, group fitness classes, pool, and Reformer Pilates.

As a PLACE member, you'll benefit from ongoing support and motivation from our dedicated team, helping you build a happier, more active lifestyle. New gym members also receive a fully customised personal fitness program through our free BEGIN program, where our qualified trainers will tailor a plan to your individual goals.

Committing to your health with us means reducing the risk of health concerns, establishing a healthy routine, and becoming part of a welcoming community where you can make new friends and achieve your wellness goals faster. Choose the membership that suits you and get started today!

[ Complete Guide to Membership Fees ](/getmedia/328d7504-1953-4c87-877f-406fbf83a874/fees-and-charges-\(1\)_2.png)

### Wellness Membership 

UNLIMITED Reformer Pilates classes, plus full access to the gym, group fitness classes, indoor and outdoor pools, and our sauna — all included in our Wellness membership for just $29.20 per week!

[ JOIN NOW ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/register?centre_name=Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PORT-FAR-WEL)

### Full Access GOLD Membership

Full access to swimming and gym facilities including sauna and group fitness classes. Weekly direct debit of $25.60 (adult), $21.50 (concession), or $15.40 (senior 50+yrs or teen 13-16yrs). $51.00 (Family, 2 adults, up to 3 children) Mum & Bub members, this is the membership for you!

[ JOIN NOW ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/purchase_membership?centre_name=Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PLA-GGS-FA-DD)

### Gym & Group Fitness Membership

Access to all gym and fitness facilities including group fitness classes. Weekly direct debit of $21.50 (adult), $18.50 (concession). or $43.40 (family 2 adults, 3 children)

[ JOIN NOW ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/purchase_membership?centre_name=Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PLA-HCGF-DD)

### Swim Only Membership

Full access to swimming and sauna facilities. Weekly direct debit of: $12.70 (adult) $8.80 (child 3-15yrs) or $24.50 (family, 2 adults, 3 children)

[ JOIN NOW ](https://blau.activeworld.com.au/purchase_membership?centre_name=Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre&for_what=membership&mpc_code=PLA-AM-AA-DD)

## 

## Getting Started is Easy!

Our memberships are powered by innovative technology. The Active World app was specifically designed to improve communication and interaction between our members and our team.

Become a member of our centre by joining below or downloading the app and using the code **PORTLAND**

Your **self managed** personal portal will enable you to:

  * Manage personal and billing details 
  * Manager your account details 
  * Update your payment details 
  * Check for your next payment 
  * Buy a new membership or visit pass
  * Scan in using a digital access card – for when you forget your pass! 
  * Book into your Group Fitness Classes 
  * View upcoming classes 
  * Send and receive messages to the Centre staff 

Learn more about your membership app [here](/venue/active-world)




#### Watch our short video on how to get started!

Download the app to login or sign up - use the code **PORTLAND

# About Us

## 

## Gym, Swimming, Sauna and Group Fitness Classes

The Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre (PLACE) aims to provide an enjoyable experience for the whole community, both members or guests to participate and use any of our services, programs and activities. We offer the largest Swimming and Water Safety program in the area helping kids Learn to Swim all year round.

The Health Club has a large gym facility which is fully equipped with a variety of weights, machines and cardio equipment. We also have numerous Group Fitness Classes per week!

PLACE has something for the whole family to enjoy, whether it be a leisurely day around one of our four swimming pools or enjoying coffee with friends after your workout. We look forward to offering you the best health and leisure experience possible. 

Come in and visit us today to see what PLACE has to offer you!

### Fitness Facilities

The fully air conditioned Gym at PLACE provides modern cardio equipment, a functional training area, and a variety of resistance machines and free weights equipment.

[ Learn more ](/train/fitness-facilities)

### Group Fitness

Getting started in a health club can be daunting and our popular group fitness classes are a great way to help build your confidence. 

[ Learn more ](/train/group-fitness-classes)

### Personal Training

Personal training is an ideal way to kick-start your training at our health club. Boost your motivation and reach your personal health and wellness goals.

[ Learn more ](/train/personal-training)

### Aquatic Facilities

A 50 metre Olympic pool, 25m indoor 25m pool, indoor programs pool, outdoor learners pool, sauna are all available at PLACE.

[ Learn more ](/swim/aquatic-facilities)

### School Programs

We run a comprehensive school swimming program to ensure kids are getting in and familiar with the water from a young age.

[ Learn more ](/learn-to-swim/school-swimming-program)

### Aqua Aerobics

Using the resistance of water automatically increases the intensity of your workout, helping to increase your strength, flexibility and your overall health.

[ Learn more ](/swim/aqua-aerobics)

### TripAdvisor Panel

# About Us

## 

## Gym, Swimming, Sauna and Group Fitness Classes

The Portland Leisure and Aquatic Centre (PLACE) aims to provide an enjoyable experience for the whole community, both members or guests to participate and use any of our services, programs and activities. The Health Club has a large gym facility which is fully equipped with a variety of weights, machines and cardio equipment. We also have numerous Group Fitness Classes per week!

PLACE has something for the whole family to enjoy, whether it be a leisurely day around one of our four swimming pools or enjoying coffee with friends after your workout. We look forward to offering you the best health and leisure experience possible. 

Come in and visit us today to see what PLACE has to offer you!

# Getting to PLACE

## Location

  
We are conveniently located at:

**22 Bentinck Street, Portland, VIC, 3305**  
  
Free car parking available at the centre.

For all general enquiries, assistance, help or support, please use the contact us form or call us on **5521 4174.**

##   
Carpark Safety

When you visit, please consider the following. 

  * Maintain a maximum speed of 10 kilometres per hour (kph) within the carpark. 

  * Exercise caution by watching for pedestrians, other vehicles and children. 

  * Take note of designated parking areas for individuals with disabilities, limited mobility and adhere to time restriction limits. 

  * If you are a tradesperson with a longer vehicle and/or trailer, where possible, please utilise parking closer to the oval area. 

  * A Taxi and School Bus Drop-off & Pickup area is designated at the front entrance of the facility. Please ensure you park your car clear of this area, and within the designated white lines. 




Your cooperation in adhering to these safety measures will help make our car park a secure and safe environment for everyone. 

  
  
**Contact Information:**  
  
**p:**[(03) 5521 7174](tel:03 5521 7174)  
**e:​**[portland@belgravialeisure.com.au](mailto:portland@belgravialeisure.com.au)

  * Learn to Swim
  * School Swimming Program 



# School Swimming Program

## School Swimming Program

The centre offers a wide range of programs for your group or school to be a part of. You can choose from end of term activities through to programs that are energised, alternative and or educational.  
  
We offer school swimming program options that are available and aligned with education requirements for water safety. Programs can be tailored to meet the school's requirements for timetabling, logistics, affordability and curriculum objectives. 

## Session Times 

The aquatics coordinator will work with organisations to discuss, plan and implement suitable programs to meet their school’s needs. Ensuring everyone has fun in a safe and friendly environment.   
  
Program times may vary depending on the duration, number of students, financial considerations and educational needs. 

## School Swimming Program Enquiries

Swimming is an essential and life-saving skill that you have for life. To enquire about our school programs please complete an enquiry form on our contact page and a team member will be in touch regarding your enquiry.

## The Curriculum

We offer a wide range of programs for your group or school to be a part of. The curriculum provides a comprehensive educational framework that enhances knowledge, skill and understanding of safer aquatic participation.   
  
The curriculum ensures alignment with and support of learning outcomes and drowning prevention strategies including:

  * The Federal Government's Curriculum Framework Guide. Where the focus is on experiential rather than command teaching. 
  * The World Health Organisation (WHO) Drowning Prevention Implementation Guide a central documented that is acknowledged worldwide. 
  * The Australian Water Safety Council's Water Safety Plan.
  * AUSTSWIM Learning Pillars Framework is a guiding document for program development, lessons planning and teaching.

# Your Membership App

## 

[DOWNLOAD THE APP NOW](http://qrco.de/bbRx0F)

## 

We believe all our members health & fitness journey should be powered by innovative technology. The Active World app was specifically designed to improve your experience with us! The app will give you greater control of your membership and our programs offered in Centre! 

The Active World app allows you to link your family memberships to manage from the once account and will give you greater visibility of your progress and achievements when visiting us! 

Our staff are here to help! Active World is built to improve communication with our team – so if you need us, we are a click of a button away to start chatting! 

Download the app today to get started and bring your membership into the palm of your hand! 

## 

  
Your Active World self-managed portal will allow you to: 

  * Manage your account details 

  * Update your payment details 

  * Check for your next payment 

  * Buy a new membership 

  * Buy a visit pass 

  * Scan in using a digital access card – for when you forget your pass! 

  * Book into your Group Fitness Classes 

  * View upcoming classes 

  * Advise of us of your GOswim non-attendance and book make-up lessons 

  * Track your GOswim learning pathways and progression 

  * Send and receive messages to the Centre staff 




What our short video on all the things Active World will allow you to do! 

  
Download the app to login or sign up - use the code **PORTLAND**

[Download the app](http://qrco.de/bbRx0F)

## 

### GET STARTED AS AN EXISITING MEMBER 

As an existing member, we have set you up using the email you provided us upon joining – **all you have to do is reset your password!**

If you are currently using Active World for your GOswim lessons – all you need to do is update the app! 

1\. [Download ](http://qrco.de/bbRx0F)the Active World App 

2\. Use the facility code **PORTLAND**

3\. Select **forgot password** to reset your account – follow the prompts 

4\. Login once ready and create your quick access code – 4 digits 

5\. Now you're in! Check your programs or book into a new class! 

  
Watch this quick video on how to set up your app 

### GET STARTED AS A NEW MEMBER 

Looking to join our community! WELCOME! 

It's super easy to get you started! 

1\. [Download ](http://qrco.de/bbRx0F)the Active World App and select Sign Up  
  
2\. Use the facility code **PORTLAND**

3\. Create your quick access code – 4 digits 

4\. Now you're in! 

5\. Click Book/Buy - Select your preference 

6\. Follow the prompts to get started! 

For more information about specific memberships or class bookings see our FAQs below. 

Watch this quick video on how to join! 

##  Frequently Asked Questions Expand all 

#####  Does the App work on iPhones and Android? 

Yes, it sure does! You can download the Active World App from the App Store or the Google Store.

[Download App ](http://qrco.de/bbRx0F)

If you are using a different device, you can login to your portal view the web link here https://blau.activeworld.com.au/

#####  I am creating an account, but it says an account already exists. 

If you are already a member with us, we have set you up using the email you provided us upon joining – all you have to do is reset your password!

This means once you reset your password and login all your membership information will be ready for you to check!

#####  How do I book into a GOswim class? 

To book yourself or your child into a GOswim lesson all you need to do is select Book/Buy from your apps home screen. Select book a GOswim lesson, you will then be asked to select the person you wish to book into that lesson. If you or your child is already in a class, it will show you available classes to book a make up lesson. If you are not current member of GOswim, you will be asked some questions on your swim ability then recommended a class to enrol into. At this stage you will need to buy a new membership to book the class. The app will take you through the process.

#####  How do I book into an Aqua Aerobics Class? 

To book yourself into an Aqua Aerobics session all you need to do is select Book/Buy from your apps home screen. Select book a class, you will then be asked to select the person you wish to book into that class. If your membership includes access to classes, you will be able to see all classes available and book in. If you are not current member, you will need to go back a step and BUY a membership to book a class.

#####  My children’s memberships are not showing in my account. 

If you have multiple memberships with us in the centre – this could be yourself and your children, you should be able to see them within your account. If you cannot, please talk to our team next time you are in the centre or message us on the app to check the email address you have used to login is the primary email on all your memberships. If your child is not currently a member, you can sign them up in the app.

#####  Can I add my partner or a relative to my account? 

Yes, you can! If you would like to share your child's GOswim or other program progress with a family member, you can add them as a relative. From the home screen of the app, click on the 3 lines in the top left-hand corner (next to our centre logo). This will bring up the task bar on the left of your screen. Now select “MY RELATIVES” - you are able to view, add or remove relatives. Once added to your profile, the relative can download the app onto their phone and login using the same information on the relative profile (the email address you used). They will be able to see everything except personal details and account information

#####  How do I contact the centre on the app? 

We have made sure that we are only the click of a button away should you need to contact us! All you have to do is select “MESSENGER” from the home screen or the task bar to chat with our team.

#####  How do I update my billing details? 

We understand billing details need to be easy to update and change! So, we have made it simple! From the home screen of the app, click on the 3 lines in the top left-hand corner (next to our centre logo). This will bring up the task bar on the left of your screen. Select “MY BILLING DETAILS” to see your current information. Select “EDIT” at the top of any section you wish to update your details in – don't forget to hit SAVE!

#####  What are ‘My Awards’? 

Awards are given when you or your child reach a milestone! Mostly used in our GOswim program, you or your child will be able to see all the achievements and what they can work towards!

#####  What is ‘Pathway’? 

The Pathway feature will give you a map view of how far you or your child have come in thier GOswim program! It will show you what levels are next and what learning outcomes need to be achieved to progress.

#####  My email address has changed, how do I update it? 

Login to your app and update your email address on your personal profile page.

#####  Is the app free? 

It sure is!

#####  I just changed my class day/time however the app has our original day/time listed. 

The App and Active World sync in live time. If your class day is showing incorrectly in your schedule, please contact the centre to ensure you are booked into the correct class.

#####  My App doesn’t show the update. 

Anyone with an IOS (Apple) you just need to update your device.

If you don't have auto update selected Go to APP Store -> Click Today (Bottom Left Hand Side) -> Click your profile pic (top right hand side) -> scroll down to active world app and click update.
